indifferentlie ſalbe decydit befoir lordis ye seſſioun secund ſpoliatioū ſay done becauſe landis poſſeſſioūis debatabill groundit fee heritage vpone ſpoliatioun lordis seſſioun ſall ꝓceid thus ſay
